This tire center has staffing issues I think, it can take some time for you to get help. It's worse when there's already a line, but you should be okay as long as you set up appointments. Service time has been pretty good, and you can kill time by shopping inside Costco and grabbing some food. Staff is friendly, shop is clean, and definitely less crowded than some other tire centers I've visited.< /text>

<Review>I can't speak to the quality of the food, as this post is primarily in regards to this establishment's service and treatment of is guests. I visited the restaurant for brunch with my boyfriend on Superbowl Sunday earlier this year, and - although the restaurant was a bit full - we were seated by the host within a couple of minutes after checking in. Once they seated us, one of the bussers came to offer us water, and after that, everything went downhill. We were literally *never* approached by a waiter to come take our orders (despite repeated attempts to get the staff's attention), and we had started there waiting to be seen at our table for over 40 minutes. They even seated a party next to us (same two-person size), took their orders, and had them served before we finally were so fed up with their clearly intentional avoidance that we left. During the entire time we were patiently waiting to be attended to, we noticed that other tables that had been served had issues with either the bill they were charged or the food they had received (some combination of wrong orders and unsatisfying food quality). The only reason I can think of as to why they never served us is that we were the only patrons of color in the entire restaurant at that time, and I truly felt like we were being singled out for it as if I had gone back in time to the civil rights era. Maybe the food is good, but the terrible, seemingly discriminatory service really should be reason enough not to come here. I would not recommend to anyone who values their time or being treated with respect, and would never return on principle. Even if the issue was just one incompetent employee that was ill- equipped to do his job, I fault management as well for allowing this kind of behavior and poor, inconsistent customer service standards along its employees.</Review>< pictures>

<UserId.>118063098615605409784< /UserId.>< review>
Highly recommended for date night or birthday!

Great location, fantastic drink selection, and the food really hits the spot. The staff is friendly and attentive, albeit a little overwhelmed. I stopped by for the Taco Tuesday and the tacos did not disappoint. The portions are generous, the meat is cooked perfectly, and each has their unique flavor with assorted toppings (al pastor came with fresh pineapple cubes!). The side salad with vinaigrette was a bit underwhelming though the tomatoes were very fresh. A side of french fries rounded out the meal, not over seasoned and hot out of the kitchen. Of drinks I recommend their signature Rye Tai, a craft beer from their selection (I'll take Allagash or Artifex), or a Pacifico with lime to make Taco Tuesday complete.

This restaurant's location is almost unbeatable. Located at the bottom of Del Mar right across the street from the San Clemente Pier. With shops and tourist traps surrounding the Pierside patio you'll get a bird's eye view of activity at one of the most popular destinations in southern California, not to mention a breathtaking view of the sunset behind the island offshore.

Food: 9/10
Drink: 10/10
Environment: 10/10
Staff: 9/10< /review>

<Text>I had the single worst restaurant experience of my life at this restaurant. It was so bad it resulted in me calling the police.

My wife, mother, and I arrived at about 1:30, and were told by a young hostess that we would need to wait. So we ordered drinks and waited for an hour. The hostess never said anything to us during this time. We never informed that we could sit inside with our dog. We were left alone to sit for an hour.

At the end of the hour, I went inside to check our table, at which point we were told that we couldn't eat there anymore because the kitchen was closed. This was clearly a huge error on the part of Pierside. We asked to talk to the manager, at which point Owner/Manager Keon Nayebdadash appeared to talk to us.

<Review>If you could bring a C+ to life, Pierside would be it's physical form.
They have entr√©es they CAN charge more for, but they execute them with the bland beckiness of a Sysco delivery truck. The fish is frozen as are the hamburger patties...they taste fine and all but it's no secret to your tongue. The "wasabi" soba noodles under the ahi might as well be tossed in mayo... If that's not already what they do.
The one drink I had was the weekly special... a dragon fruit tequila cocktail which sounded great... But like the soba noodles... Tasted uninspired and fell flat.
It makes me wonder if the whole point is to keep from scaring away the local Beckies with too much flavor in fear of being labeled "ethnic"

Server was kind though. Loved her.<//Review>< pictures>

< Text>
What do you crave?  What makes a great Restaurant? What do you look for when choosing a "Place to eat"? Biggest Portions?  Lowest price?  Biggest buffet or maybe who has the best deal on a pitcher or Lucky Lager?

Dining Experience.  When I go out I want it to do something for me.

Pierside makes me fee good.
Love this place. I leave satisfied each time.
If I am having just an appetizer and a craft beer.
Filet  and wine.?

Pierside you watch the sun setting over the pacific and listen to the live music and all of the friendly chatter and laughter.
The food is excellent. craft beer o-plenty
Comfortable and casual.

There are Restaurants and then there are Bars.
Pierside is home.  Welcome back.

The Friendly service has awesome recommendations depending on your personal taste and mood.
When I walk in I am asked how I feel and what I am in the mood for.
If I was hot and said I need something lite and cool.
Well I let them choose for me.  And the Seared Ahi Salad arrives to accompany My very refreshing drink.  Which I have to give Scuba Steve credit on this one and many others.  Ask for the #ScubaTea It really tastes like tea but with a wobble.
The Seared Ahi is no longer a menu item but if we all ask Keon to bring back the Ahi it will make it a perfect day
Order yourself a drink called #TheScubaTea

Be sure to tell them G. Douglas Sent you.

#bestcraftbeer
#icecoldbrew
#piersidebar
#livemusic
#sunsetdining
#sanclementerestaurants</Text>

< Review>
We have been taking our dog to Companions for approximately 3 years now and in that time they have dealt with several issues that were age related.  Because of their knowledge and compassion, our dog lived longer and better than what we thought was possible given the medical conditions she had.  Dr. Duffy was our dogs normal vet-she is professional yet really loves animals... she made appointments easier on our dog than any other vet that she had in her 15 years of life.

In the last few weeks, it became clear that our dogs quality of life was suffering.  We made the difficult decision to have her put to sleep. The appointment went as smooth as it possibly could have. We saw Dr. Caruso on a few occasions over the years and she is the one that ended up putting our dog to sleep.  It was a relief to have a vet who didn't care how many biscuits our dog ate while she was shaving her arm and administering the medicine...as long as our dog was comfortable and stress free, that was all that mattered.  Our dog, who was very food driven up to her last day, went to sleep with biscuits in her mouth.

We couldn't recommend Companions any more highly.  The staff have been helpful over the years-making sure medications could be filled at the drop of a hat and appointments were scheduled quickly and conveniently.  Both Drs. Duffy and Caruso have great bedside manner, on top of wisdom as to the best route to take with strange health problems of an animal that can't communicate what they are feeling.  We can't thank them enough for the care they provided for our dog, especially in the hardest years of her life!<//Review>

<Review>Why 4 stars? Because it's quick, cheap and convenient.

---   ---   ---

This is one of the closest physical eateries to my office when I'm in SF, so it was only a matter of time before I tried it out. And when I see a prosciutto and mozzarella sandwich on any menu, it's very unlikely that I am going to choose anything besides that.

I've certainly had better prosciutto and mozzarella sandwiches before, but I enjoyed it. What I enjoyed even more was that it was probably less from 100 steps from office to sandwich and that it came in at $16.91 for the sammy + chips and a drink. In SF, that's a super cheap lunch.

I'm sure I will be back many times during future work lunches.<//Review>< Rate>

Love their chicken salad sandwich and Caesar salads. The Caesar dressing used is pretty light for what you are normally used to, and it's awesome.

Salads are huge, and will definitely fill you up.

Place can get super busy during lunch hour, so try to come in during off-peak hours if at all possible.
